            <text>Two masses M and m (M>m) are connected by strings as pulley system. The acceleration is:</text>
            <option id="A">(M-m)g/(M+m)</option>
            <option id="B">(M+m)g/(M-m)</option><option id="C">Mg/m</option><option id="D">g</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>a = Net Pulling Force / Total Mass = (Mg - mg) / (M+m).</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A 50kg man stands on a scale in a lift accelerating down at 2 m/s^2. Reading is (g=10):</text>
            <option id="A">400N</option>
            <option id="B">500N</option>
            <option id="C">600N</option>
            <option id="D">300N</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Apparent weight = m(g-a) = 50(10-2) = 400N.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A car of mass 1000kgNegotiates a banked curve of radius 90m on a frictionless road. If the banking angle is 45 degrees, the speed of the car is:</text>
            <option id="A">10 m/s</option>
            <option id="B">20 m/s</option>
            <option id="C">30 m/s</option>
            <option id="D">5 m/s</option>
            <answer>C</answer>
            <explanation>v = sqrt(rg tan theta) = sqrt(90 * 10 * 1) = 30.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A force of 10N acts on a body of mass 2kg for 3 seconds. The impulse is:</text>

            <option id="D">6 Ns</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Impulse = F * t = 10 * 3 = 30.</explanation>
        </question>

            <option id="D">0N</option>
            <answer>B</answer>

        <question>
            <text>A monkey of mass 40kg climbs on a rope which can stand a max tension of 600N. In which case will the rope break? (g=10)</text>
            <option id="A">Climbs up with a = 6 m/s^2</option>
            <option id="B">Climbs down with a = 4 m/s^2</option>
            <option id="C">Climbs up with v = 5 m/s</option>
            <option id="D">Falls down freely</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>T = m(g+a). 40(10+6) = 640N > 600N. Break.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A block of mass m is kept on a wedge of mass M. To keep the block stationary wrt wedge, acceleration of wedge is:</text>
            <option id="A">g tan theta</option>
            <option id="B">g cot theta</option>
            <option id="C">g sin theta</option>
            <option id="D">g cos theta</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Pseudo force ma. ma cos = mg sin. a = g tan theta.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A particle slides down a smooth hemisphere from the top. It leaves contact at height h. h is:</text>
            <option id="A">2R/3</option>
            <option id="B">R/3</option>
            <option id="C">R/2</option>
            <option id="D">R</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>mg cos - N = mv^2/R. At leave, N=0. cos = h/R. v^2 = 2g(R-h). g(h/R) = 2g(R-h)/R. h = 2R - 2h. 3h=2R.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>Two blocks A and B of masses 3m and m are connected by a string. Whole system is suspended by a spring. String is cut. Acceleration of A and B?</text>
            <option id="A">A: g/3 up, B: g down</option>
            <option id="B">A: g up, B: g down</option>
            <option id="C">A: g/3 down, B: g up</option>
            <option id="D">A: g up, B: g up</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Spring force kx = 4mg. String cut. Force on B is only mg down -> g. Force on A is kx - 3mg = 4mg - 3mg = mg (up). a = mg/3m = g/3 up.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>Three blocks A, B, C of equal mass m are placed one over the other on a smooth horizontal surface. Coeff of friction between any two blocks is u. Max Force F on lowermost block C so that they move together?</text>
            <option id="A">3umg</option>
            <option id="B">umg</option>
            <option id="C">2umg</option>
            <option id="D">6umg</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Limiting friction is between A and B (requires least force to slip). f_max = umg. For A, ma = umg -> a_max = ug. For whole system, F = (3m)a_max = 3mug.</explanation>
        </question>

            <answer>A</answer>

    <hard>
        <!-- 40 HARD QUESTIONS -->
        <question>
            <text>A solid sphere is rolling on a surface with friction coefficient u. Force F acts at center. Max F for pure rolling?</text>
            <option id="A">7/2 umg</option>
            <option id="B">5/2 umg</option>
            <option id="C">umg</option>
            <option id="D">7umg</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>f = F - ma. Torque fR = I alpha = 2/5 mR^2 (a/R). f = 2/5 ma. F - 2/5 ma = ma. F = 1.4 ma. f <= umg. 2/5 ma <= umg. ma <= 2.5 umg. F = 1.4 * 2.5 umg = 3.5 umg = 7/2 umg.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A rod of mass m and length l is struck at one end by a force F perpendicular to rod for short time t. Velocity of center of mass?</text>
            <option id="A">Ft / m</option>
            <option id="B">Ft / 2m</option>
            <option id="C">Ft</option><option id="D">Zero</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Impulse J = Ft. J = m v_cm.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>Angular velocity of rod in previous question?</text>
            <option id="A">6Ft / ml</option>
            <option id="B">12Ft / ml</option>
            <option id="C">3Ft / ml</option>
            <option id="D">Ft / ml</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Angular Impulse J(l/2) = I w. F t l / 2 = (ml^2/12) w. w = 6Ft / ml.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A disc of radius R spins with w and is gently placed on a rough horizontal surface. Time after which pure rolling starts?</text>
            <option id="A">Rw / 3ug</option>
            <option id="B">Rw / ug</option>
            <option id="C">Rw / 2ug</option>
            <option id="D">2Rw / ug</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>v = at = ug t. w' = w - alpha t = w - (2ug/R)t. v = Rw' condition. ugt = R(w - 2ugt/R) = Rw - 2ugt. 3ugt = Rw. t = Rw/3ug.</explanation>
        </question>
        <question>
            <text>A ladder leans against a smooth wall. The floor is rough. Minimum angle theta with horizontal to not slip?</text>
            <option id="A">tan theta = 1/2u</option><option id="B">tan theta = 1/u</option><option id="C">tan theta = 2u</option><option id="D">tan theta = u</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>Torque balance. mg(L/2 cos) = N_wall (L sin). N_wall = mg/2 cot. N_floor = mg. f = N_wall <= u N_floor. mg/2 cot <= u mg. cot <= 2u. tan >= 1/2u.</explanation>
        </question>

        <question><text>Solid sphere rolling on curved track radius R.             <option id="B">7 J</option><option id="C">5 J</option><option id="D">-5 J</option>
            <answer>A</answer>
            <explanation>W_ext = - W_field. F_field = mE. W_field = F.d = (2i+3j).(2i+j) = 4+3=7. W_ext = -7 (against field). BUT Potential diff V_f - V_i = - Int E.dr. Delta U = m Delta V. If we move against field, we do +work? Work done "by field" is 7J. Work done "to move" usually implies external agent, which is -7J. Wait. Force on particle is F. To move it, we apply -F.         <question>

            <answer>A</answer><explanation>P2 > P1. Pressure is higher in smaller bubble. Radius of interface R = r1r2/(r1-r2). Concave towards smaller.</explanation>

        <question>
            <text>Efficiency of Carnot engine 40%. To increase to 50%, increase source T by dH or decrease sink T by dL. Relation?</text>
            <option id="A">dH > dL usually? Need check.</option><option id="B">dH = dL</option><option id="C">dH < dL</option><option id="D">None</option>
            <answer>A</answer><explanation>eta = 1 - T2/T1. 0.4 -> 0.5. 0.6 = T2/T1. 0.5 = T2' / T1 or T2/T1'. Case 1: T2' = 0.5 T1. dL = 0.6T1 - 0.5T1 = 0.1T1. Case 2: 0.5 = 0.6T1 / T1'. T1' = 1.2 T1. dH = 0.2 T1. dH (0.2T1) > dL (0.1T1). So dH > dL. Easier to decrease sink.</explanation>
        </question>

            <text>According to MOT, HOMO of N2 is?</text>
            <option id="A">Sigma 2pz</option><option id="B">Pi 2px</option><option id="C">Sigma 2s</option><option id="D">Pi star</option>
            <answer>A</answer><explanation>Sigma-2p crossing effect (N2). 2121. Wait. Order: Sig1s, Sig*1s, Sig2s, Sig*2s, Pi2p=Pi2p, Sig2pz.
            Correction: For N2, Sigma 2pz is HIGHER than Pi 2p? 
            Order up to 14e: Sig1s < * < Sig2s < * < Pi(x,y) < Sigma(z).
            So HOMO is Sigma 2pz. Correct.</explanation>

            <text>Volume of 0.1M KMnO4 required to oxidize 100ml 0.1M FeSO4 in acid?</text>
            <option id="A">20 ml</option><option id="B">100 ml</option><option id="C">50 ml</option><option id="D">10 ml</option>
            <answer>A</answer><explanation>N1V1=N2V2. Mn change 5. Fe change 1.
            Normality KMnO4: 0.1*5 = 0.5N.
            Normality FeSO4: 0.1*1 = 0.1N.
            0.5 * V = 0.1 * 100
            V = 10 / 0.5 = 20 ml.</explanation>
        </question>

            <answer>A</answer><explanation>Complex balancing. As (+3 -> +5)x2=4. S(-2 -> +6)x3=24. Total ox 28. N (+5 -> +2) change 3.
            Factor 3 (As2S3) and 28 (NO3). 3 As2S3 + 28 NO3- ...</explanation>

        <question>
            <text>For cell Zn|Zn2+(C1) || Zn2+(C2)|Zn. E > 0 if:</text>
            <option id="A">C2 > C1</option><option id="B">C1 > C2</option><option id="C">C1 = C2</option><option id="D">Never</option>
            <answer>A</answer><explanation>Concentration cell. Spontaneous from low to high conc? No.
            Zn -> Zn2+(C1) + 2e. Zn2+(C2) + 2e -> Zn. Net: Zn2+(C2) -> Zn2+(C1).
            Q = C1/C2. E = -0.059/2 log(C1/C2).
            For E > 0, log(C1/C2) must be negative. C1/C2 < 1. C1 < C2.
            So C2 > C1.</explanation>
        </question>
